    <div id="description" class="markdown description col7">
        
        <div id="description-text">
            This is 24&quot; tall by 17&quot; wide 2 pieces assembled together for the 2 dimensional look.<br /><br />Both pieces are cut from 18 gauge steel and powder coated for a long lasting finish.<br /><br />We recommend using picture hanging wire to hang. <br /><br />This was a custom request designed by MetalArtDesignz<br /><br />Also larger option available        </div>
                    <div id="shop-about" class="ui-toolkit">
                <div class="text-center">
    <h2 class="text-body-largest strong">        Meet <span>the</span> owner <span>of</span> <a href="https://www.etsy.com/shop/MetalArtDesignz?ref=l2-about-shopname">MetalArtDesignz</a>
    </h2>
            <a href="https://www.etsy.com/shop/MetalArtDesignz?ref=l2-more-about#about" class="display-block text-gray-darker text-body">
                    Learn more about the shop and process
    
        </a>
    
            <div class="display-inline-block mt-xs-3 mr-xs-5 ml-xs-5">
                        <a href="https://www.etsy.com/shop/MetalArtDesignz/about?ref=l2-about" class="display-block text-gray-lightest">
                        <img src='https://img0.etsystatic.com/046/0/9534724/isc_190x190.17044636514_qhr6.jpg' width=190 height=190 class='circle width-100px height-100px' alt='' />

                            <div class="ui-toolkit shop-faqs-container">
                <h2 class="pt-xs-3 pb-xs-2 text-center text-body-largest strong">Frequently asked questions about MetalArtDesignz</h2>
    <div class="shop-faq-panel panel bt-xs-1 bl-xs-0 bb-xs-0 br-xs-0 mb-xs-0">
        <div class="panel-body pl-xs-0 pr-xs-0" data-faq-id="101795678714">
            <div class="shop-faq-accordion accordion accordion-panel accordion-has-icon">
                <input type="checkbox" id="faq-accordion-0" class="accordion-state">
                <label for="faq-accordion-0" class="accordion-label">
                    <a class="text-gray" data-region="faq-question-text">What is raw metal?</a>
                </label>
                <div class="accordion-body">
                    <div class="pt-xs-3 faq-answer text-gray-lighter" data-region="faq-answer-text">
                        Raw metal is just, raw metal with no coating which will rust over time may arrive with sharp edges and small metal shaving remnants from sanding
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="shop-faq-panel panel bt-xs-1 bl-xs-0 bb-xs-0 br-xs-0 mb-xs-0">
        <div class="panel-body pl-xs-0 pr-xs-0" data-faq-id="104880196237">
            <div class="shop-faq-accordion accordion accordion-panel accordion-has-icon">
                <input type="checkbox" id="faq-accordion-1" class="accordion-state">
                <label for="faq-accordion-1" class="accordion-label">
                    <a class="text-gray" data-region="faq-question-text">What is the difference between raw and powder coated metal?</a>
                </label>
                <div class="accordion-body">
                    <div class="pt-xs-3 faq-answer text-gray-lighter" data-region="faq-answer-text">
                        Raw metal will rust. Powder coated will not it is applied with electrostatic charge and then baked on in an oven
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>

        js.src = '//c.go-mpulse.net/boomerang/' +
        'QNSRX-CQ5ZY-DYD42-85SLW-KYDW3';
        BOOMR_lstart=new Date().getTime();
        this.body.appendChild(js);
      };
      doc.write('<body onload="document._l();">');
      doc.close();
  } catch (e) {
    /**
     * 2016-04-07 [dna]: doc.open()._l has given us a significant amount of clientlogger error spam
     * lately because doc.open() is undefined for specific listings. Our best guess is some sort of botnet, but this should
     * stop those errors without meaningfully impacting mpulse.
     */
  }
})(window.Etsy);
</script>
